    for (i = 0; i < locations.length; i++) {

        marker = new google.maps.Marker({
            position: new google.maps.LatLng(locations[i][1], locations[i][2]),
            map: map,
            html: locations[0],
        });

        google.maps.event.addListener(marker, 'click', (function (marker, i) {
            //marker.setIcon('http://192.168.1.88/hedinbil_se/wp-content/themes/twentytwelve/img/mark.png?chst=d_map_pin_letter&chld='+i+'|FFFFFF|FFFFFF');

                infowindow.setContent(locations[i][0]);

                infowindow.open(map, marker);

            }

        })(marker, i));

    }

   jQuery(document).ready(function () {

		jQuery(document).on('click', 'body.home ul.marke li label', function() {
			var brand = jQuery(this).find("span").text();
			var params = {"brandName": brand, action: "get_modell"}
			$.post("https://www.hedinbil.se/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php", params, function (data) {
				if (data) {
					jQuery("#modell").html(data);
				}
			});
			jQuery("#modell-select").css({"display":"block","opacity":"1.0","-webkit-box-shadow": "0px 0px 5px 0px #999","-moz-box-shadow": "0px 0px 5px 0px #999","box-shadow": "0px 0px 5px 0px #999"});
			/*jQuery("#modell-select select").css({"border-left-color":"#ffffff"});*/
			setTimeout(function(){jQuery("#modell-select").css({"box-shadow":"none"});},300);
		});
        jQuery(document).on('click', 'body.home ul.marke2 li label', function() {
			var brand = jQuery(this).parent("li").find("#brandid").text();
			var params = {"brandID": brand, action: "get_modell_transport"}
			$.post("https://www.hedinbil.se/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php", params, function (data2) {
				if (data2) {
					jQuery("#modell2").html(data2);
				}
			});
			jQuery("#modell-select2").css({"display":"block","opacity":"1.0","-webkit-box-shadow": "0px 0px 5px 0px #999","-moz-box-shadow": "0px 0px 5px 0px #999","box-shadow": "0px 0px 5px 0px #999"});
			/*jQuery("#modell-select2 select").css({"border-left-color":"#ffffff"});*/
			setTimeout(function(){jQuery("#modell-select2").css({"box-shadow":"none"});},300);

		});

        function ajax_load() {
            var values = new Array();
            $.each($("input[name='filtering[]']:checked"), function () {
                values.push($(this).val());
            });
            var params = {"selected_post": values, action: "load_more"}
            $.post("https://www.hedinbil.se/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php", params, function (data) {
                if (data) {
                    $('#owlcarousel_annonsering2').html(data);
                    $(' #owlcarousel_annonsering2').owlCarousel({
                        nav: true, items: 3,
                        loop: true,
                        autoplay: true,
                        navigation: true,
                        responsiveClass: true,
                        autoplayHoverPause: true,
                        responsive: {
                            0: {
                                items: 1,
                                nav: true
                            },
                            640: {
                                items: 2,
                                nav: false
                            },
                            768: {
                                items: 3,
                                nav: true,
                                loop: true
                            }
                        }
                    });

                }
            });
        }

    });
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   jQuery(document).ready(function() {
      /* mobile menu
    if(jQuery(window).width() < 449){
    	equal_height_slide();
	}*/
	jQuery('.caret').parent().click(function(e){
		  if(jQuery(this).hasClass('active')){
			  e.stopImmediatePropagation()
			  jQuery(this).removeClass('active')
			  jQuery(this).next().slideUp(500)
		  }else{
			  e.preventDefault()
			  jQuery(this).next().slideDown(500)
			  jQuery("#menu-main li a").removeClass('active')
			  jQuery(this).addClass('active')
			  jQuery(this).parent().siblings().find('.dropdown-menu').slideUp(500)
		  }
	});


 });

	jQuery(window).load(function($) {
		var geturl = window.location.href;
		var hash = 	geturl.split('#')[1];
		if(hash !="" && hash != undefined && hash != "undefined"){
			jQuery('html,body').animate({scrollTop: jQuery("#"+hash).offset().top},'slow');
		}

    });

	jQuery(document).on("click",".load-kampajer .two-buttons-popup .kontakta, .load-kampajer .two-buttons-popup .boka",function(e) {
		var parameter = jQuery('.fancybox-opened');
		e.preventDefault();
		jQuery('.fancybox-overlay .fancybox-wrap').css('cursor','pointer');
		jQuery(parameter).addClass('disable-popup');
		var url = 'https://www.hedinbil.se/wp-content/themes/twentytwelve';
	    var nzData = '';
	    nzData = jQuery(this).attr("data-url");
	    jQuery.ajax({
	        type: 'POST',
	        url: nzData,
	        success: function(response) {
	        	jQuery('.fancybox-opened').removeClass('disable-popup');
	            jQuery('.fancybox-inner .kampajer-popup').html('<div class="back-kampanje-car"><img src="'+url+'/img/arrow-back.jpg" alt="" /></div>'+response);
                jQuery('.fancybox-overlay .fancybox-wrap').addClass('fancybox-kontact');
	            jQuery('.fancybox-skin').append('<div class="image-loader" style="text-align: center;display: none;"><img src="'+url+'/img/Preloader_8.gif" style="width: 30px;" alt="mercedes-c-klass-sedan-1" id="thumb_img"></div>');
	        },
	        error: function() {
	            alert("Sorry ! Please try again!")
	        }
	    });
	});
	jQuery(document).on("click",".fancybox-inner .kampajer-popup .back-kampanje-car",function() {
		jQuery(this).parent().parent().parent().parent().parent().addClass('disable-popup');
	    var nzData = '';
	    nzData = 'https://www.hedinbil.se/wp-content/themes/twentytwelve/load-kampanjer.php?loadkampanjer=';
	    jQuery.ajax({
	        type: 'POST',
	        url: nzData,
	        success: function(response) {
	        	jQuery('.fancybox-opened').removeClass('disable-popup');
	            jQuery('.fancybox-inner .kampajer-popup').html(response);
	            jQuery('.fancybox-overlay .fancybox-wrap').removeClass('fancybox-kontact');
	            jQuery('.fancybox-overlay .fancybox-wrap').removeClass('fancybox-boka');
	        },
	        error: function() {
	            alert("Sorry ! Please try again!")
	        }
	    });
	});
  </script>
